<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:finale.html>finale</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">finālis</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sports.html>sports</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:finale.html>finale</a></i>.

href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(<a href class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language"><a href = vnd.unilang:welsh.html>Welsh</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">pinc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σπίγγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spíngos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chaffinch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пе́нка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pénka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = </p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saxon.html>Saxon</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">findan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*finþan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finþaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:go.html>go</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pass.html>pass</a>; <div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/170px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/255px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/340px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2336" data-file-height="3504" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boy.html>boy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:holding.html>holding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> “fishy” (<a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fish.html>fish</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:his.html>his</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hand.html>hand</a></div></div></div>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flamenco.html>flamenco</a> (36129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Vlaming</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:flamenco.html>flamenco</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:feminine.html>feminine</a> singular</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-es f | s-form-of" lang="es">flamenca</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:masculine.html>masculine</a> plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-es m | p-form-of" lang="es">flamencos</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:feminine.html>feminine</a> plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-es f | p-form-of" lang="es">flamencas</b>)
</p>
